frau, or "file raw" is an command line utility that prints a file's content under the form of a byte array literal in a specific programming language.

Ever had to embed the contents of an image or a generic file into your source code?
I certainly had to do one of these two, so i made this.

Supported languages (as of now): C, C++, C#, Java, Go, Rust, Javascript and Python\
Supported image formats (as of now): PNG, JPEG, TGA, BPM, PSD, HDR, PIC, PPM, PGM (mostly untested)

Width and height are specified separately in the output data of any image.

## Dependencies
[stb_image](https://github.com/nothings/stb) - for deciphering image data.\
[make](https://www.gnu.org/software/make/) - for building the source.\
The C standard library.

## Usage
```console
frau <file> [options]

Options:
 -lang <value>   Specifies in which language to create a byte representation of the file
                value: c (default), cpp, cs, java, go, rs, js, py

 --help  Shows this message
```

## Example
![A 16x16 pixel drawing of a heart.](docs/images/heart.png)
```console
$ frau heart.png -lang c

unsigned char bytes[256] = {
```

The first 3 sentences of Richard Nixon's resignation speech.
```console
$ frau resignation.txt -lang go
```

## Installation
```console
$ git clone https://github.com/bordeitudor/frau.git
cd frau
make
```
